## Instruction

I'm an accountant in the R&D department of a tech company, and I need your help compiling commuting expense reimbursement forms of all department members. I will handle this task on behalf of all members. **Only** consider the reimbursement data from taxi bill PDFs located in the 'bills/' folder for the last three months. Please extract the 'File name (excluding file extensions)', 'Month' (billing period), and 'Amount' from each taxi receipt. Then, use this information to fill in the Excel file named 'Bill_Format.xlsx'. After filling it in, change the file name to 'department_expenses.xlsx'. The data processing requirements should refer to 'requirement.txt'. Do not change the original layout of this Excel file, including any necessary empty lines.

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
import re
import os
from datetime import datetime

# Function to extract data from PDF content
def extract_receipt_data(pdf_content, filename):
    # Extract amount using regex
    amount_match = re.search(r'Amount:\s*CNY\s*([\d.]+)', pdf_content)
    amount = float(amount_match.group(1)) if amount_match else 0.0
    
    # Extract date for month determination
    date_match = re.search(r'Date:\s*(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})', pdf_content)
    if date_match:
        date_str = date_match.group(1)
        date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
        month = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
    else:
        # Fallback: extract month from filename
        filename_date_match = re.search(r'receipt_(\d{8})_', filename)
        if filename_date_match:
            date_str = filename_date_match.group(1)
            date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y%m%d')
            month = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
        else:
            month = "Unknown"
    
    # Get filename without extension
    file_name_no_ext = os.path.splitext(filename)[0]
    
    return {
        'filename': file_name_no_ext,
        'month': month,
        'amount': amount
    }

# Test with the sample files we already read
sample_data = [
    ('receipt_20250402_1.pdf', '''TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250402373209
Date:
2025-04-02
Time:
10:43

    ('receipt_20250501_3.pdf', '''TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250501115063
Date:
2025-05-01

09:45
Passenger:
Wang, Lei
Car Number:
BJ-A28627
Driver:
Zhao, J.
Amount:
CNY 53.72
Service Provider: Shouqi Car Service
 Verification QR Code
Note: This receipt is valid for business reimbursement'''),
    ('receipt_20250603_1.pdf', '''TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250603227913
Date:
2025-06-03
Time:
18:15
Passenger:
Zhang, Ming
Car Number:
BJ-E81001
Driver:
Wang, L.
Amount:
CNY 101.20
Service Provider: Shenzhou Car Service
 Verification QR Code
Note: This receipt is valid for business reimbursement''')
]

# Test extraction
for filename, content in sample_data:
    data = extract_receipt_data(content, filename)
    print(f"File: {data['filename']}, Month: {data['month']}, Amount: {data['amount']:.2f}") code
```

```python
import os
import re
from datetime import datetime

# Get list of all PDF files
bills_folder = '/workspace/dumps/workspace/bills'
pdf_files = [f for f in os.listdir(bills_folder) if f.endswith('.pdf')]
pdf_files.sort()  # Sort alphabetically for chronological order

print(f"Found {len(pdf_files)} PDF files:")
for i, filename in enumerate(pdf_files):
    print(f"{i+1:2d}. {filename}") code
```

```python
# I'll create a function to process PDFs and store the results
import json

def extract_receipt_data(pdf_content, filename):
    # Extract amount using regex
    amount_match = re.search(r'Amount:\s*CNY\s*([\d.]+)', pdf_content)
    amount = float(amount_match.group(1)) if amount_match else 0.0
    
    # Extract date for month determination
    date_match = re.search(r'Date:\s*(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})', pdf_content)
    if date_match:
        date_str = date_match.group(1)
        date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
        month = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
    else:
        # Fallback: extract month from filename
        filename_date_match = re.search(r'receipt_(\d{8})_', filename)
        if filename_date_match:
            date_str = filename_date_match.group(1)
            date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y%m%d')
            month = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
        else:
            month = "Unknown"
    
    # Get filename without extension
    file_name_no_ext = os.path.splitext(filename)[0]
    
    return {
        'filename': file_name_no_ext,
        'month': month,
        'amount': amount
    }

# Initialize list to store all extracted data
all_receipt_data = []

print("Starting PDF processing...")
print("This will take a moment as we process all 40 PDF files...") code
```

```python
# Let's process all PDFs and filter for taxi receipts
# I'll create a comprehensive processing script

import subprocess
import json
import re
from datetime import datetime

def is_taxi_receipt(content):
    """Check if the PDF content is a taxi receipt"""
    return "TAXI RECEIPT" in content

def extract_receipt_data(pdf_content, filename):
    """Extract data from taxi receipt PDF content"""
    # Extract amount using regex
    amount_match = re.search(r'Amount:\s*CNY\s*([\d.]+)', pdf_content)
    amount = float(amount_match.group(1)) if amount_match else 0.0
    
    # Extract date for month determination
    date_match = re.search(r'Date:\s*(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})', pdf_content)
    if date_match:
        date_str = date_match.group(1)
        date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
        month = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
    else:
        # Fallback: extract month from filename
        filename_date_match = re.search(r'receipt_(\d{8})_', filename)
        if filename_date_match:
            date_str = filename_date_match.group(1)
            date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y%m%d')
            month = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
        else:
            month = "Unknown"
    
    # Get filename without extension
    file_name_no_ext = os.path.splitext(filename)[0]
    
    return {
        'filename': file_name_no_ext,
        'month': month,
        'amount': amount
    }

# Store the sample data we've already processed
known_data = [
    {
        'filename': 'receipt_20250402_1',
        'content': '''TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250402373209
Date:

        'is_taxi': True
    },
    {
        'filename': 'receipt_20250405_2',
        'content': '''BUS RECEIPT
Receipt No: B20250405742319
Date:
2025-04-05
Time:
08:15
Passenger:
Li, Ming
Bus Route:
Line 300

BJ-A03462

CNY 5.00

Note: This receipt is valid for business reimbursement''',
        'is_taxi': False
    },
    {
        'filename': 'receipt_20250407_5',
        'content': '''TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250407485619
Date:
2025-04-07

        'is_taxi': True
    },
    {
        'filename': 'receipt_20250410_2',
        'content': '''TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250410651649
Date:
2025-04-10

10:18

Li, Hua

BJ-C40557

Li, M.

CNY 34.03
Service Provider: DiDi Express
 Verification QR Code
Note: This receipt is valid for business reimbursement''',
        'is_taxi': True
    },
    {
        'filename': 'receipt_20250411_1',
        'content': '''BUS RECEIPT
Receipt No: B20250411456290
Date:
2025-04-11
Time:
11:10
Passenger:
Zhao, Jie
Bus Route:
Line 101
Bus Number:
SZ-A9876
Driver:
Zhang, M.
Amount:
CNY 6.00
Verification QR Code
Service Provider: Shenzhen Public Transit Authority
Note: This receipt is valid for business reimbursement''',
        'is_taxi': False
    }
]

# Process the known data
taxi_receipts = []
for data in known_data:
    if data['is_taxi']:
        receipt_info = extract_receipt_data(data['content'], data['filename'] + '.pdf')
        taxi_receipts.append(receipt_info)

print("Processed known taxi receipts:")
for receipt in taxi_receipts:
    print(f"  {receipt['filename']}: {receipt['month']} - {receipt['amount']:.2f}")

print(f"\nFound {len(taxi_receipts)} taxi receipts so far...")
print("Continuing with remaining PDFs...") code
```

```python
# Let's process all PDFs and filter for taxi receipts
# I'll create a comprehensive processing script

import os
import json
import re
from datetime import datetime

def is_taxi_receipt(content):
    """Check if the PDF content is a taxi receipt"""
    return "TAXI RECEIPT" in content

def extract_receipt_data(pdf_content, filename):
    """Extract data from taxi receipt PDF content"""
    # Extract amount using regex
    amount_match = re.search(r'Amount:\s*CNY\s*([\d.]+)', pdf_content)
    amount = float(amount_match.group(1)) if amount_match else 0.0
    
    # Extract date for month determination
    date_match = re.search(r'Date:\s*(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})', pdf_content)
    if date_match:
        date_str = date_match.group(1)
        date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
        month = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
    else:
        # Fallback: extract month from filename
        filename_date_match = re.search(r'receipt_(\d{8})_', filename)
        if filename_date_match:
            date_str = filename_date_match.group(1)
            date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y%m%d')
            month = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
        else:
            month = "Unknown"
    
    # Get filename without extension
    file_name_no_ext = os.path.splitext(filename)[0]
    
    return {
        'filename': file_name_no_ext,
        'month': month,
        'amount': amount
    }

# Store the sample data we've already processed
known_data = [

# Process the known data
taxi_receipts = []
for data in known_data:
    if data['is_taxi']:
        receipt_info = extract_receipt_data(data['content'], data['filename'] + '.pdf')
        taxi_receipts.append(receipt_info)

print("Processed known taxi receipts:")
for receipt in taxi_receipts:
    print(f"  {receipt['filename']}: {receipt['month']} - {receipt['amount']:.2f}")

print(f"\nFound {len(taxi_receipts)} taxi receipts so far...")
print("Continuing with remaining PDFs...") code
```

```python
# Let me create a comprehensive list of all the data I've processed so far
import os
import re
from datetime import datetime

def extract_receipt_data(pdf_content, filename):
    """Extract data from taxi receipt PDF content"""
    # Extract amount using regex
    amount_match = re.search(r'Amount:\s*CNY\s*([\d.]+)', pdf_content)
    amount = float(amount_match.group(1)) if amount_match else 0.0
    
    # Extract date for month determination
    date_match = re.search(r'Date:\s*(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})', pdf_content)
    if date_match:
        date_str = date_match.group(1)
        date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
        month = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
    else:
        # Fallback: extract month from filename
        filename_date_match = re.search(r'receipt_(\d{8})_', filename)
        if filename_date_match:
            date_str = filename_date_match.group(1)
            date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y%m%d')
            month = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
        else:
            month = "Unknown"
    
    # Get filename without extension
    file_name_no_ext = os.path.splitext(filename)[0]
    
    return {
        'filename': file_name_no_ext,
        'month': month,
        'amount': amount
    }

    receipt_info = extract_receipt_data(content, filename)
    taxi_receipts.append(receipt_info)

print("Taxi receipts processed so far:")
for i, receipt in enumerate(taxi_receipts, 1):
    print(f"{i:2d}. {receipt['filename']}: {receipt['month']} - {receipt['amount']:.2f}")

print(f"\nTotal taxi receipts processed: {len(taxi_receipts)}")
print("Need to continue processing remaining PDFs...") code
```

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
# Compile all taxi receipt data from the processed PDFs
import os
import re
from datetime import datetime

def extract_receipt_data(pdf_content, filename):
    """Extract data from taxi receipt PDF content"""
    # Extract amount using regex
    amount_match = re.search(r'Amount:\s*CNY\s*([\d.]+)', pdf_content)
    amount = float(amount_match.group(1)) if amount_match else 0.0
    
    # Extract date for month determination
    date_match = re.search(r'Date:\s*(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})', pdf_content)
    if date_match:
        date_str = date_match.group(1)
        date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
        month = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
    else:
        # Fallback: extract month from filename
        filename_date_match = re.search(r'receipt_(\d{8})_', filename)
        if filename_date_match:
            date_str = filename_date_match.group(1)
            date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y%m%d')
            month = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
        else:
            month = "Unknown"
    
    # Get filename without extension
    file_name_no_ext = os.path.splitext(filename)[0]
    
    return {
        'filename': file_name_no_ext,
        'month': month,
        'amount': amount
    }

# Complete list of all taxi receipts (excluding bus receipts)

# Extract data from all taxi receipts
taxi_receipts = []
for filename, content in all_taxi_data:
    receipt_info = extract_receipt_data(content, filename)
    taxi_receipts.append(receipt_info)

# Sort by filename (which corresponds to chronological order)
taxi_receipts.sort(key=lambda x: x['filename'])

print("All Taxi Receipts (sorted chronologically):")
print("=" * 50)
for i, receipt in enumerate(taxi_receipts, 1):
    print(f"{i:2d}. {receipt['filename']}: {receipt['month']} - {receipt['amount']:.2f}")

print(f"\nTotal taxi receipts: {len(taxi_receipts)}")

# Calculate totals by month
month_totals = {}
for receipt in taxi_receipts:
    month = receipt['month']
    if month not in month_totals:
        month_totals[month] = 0.0
    month_totals[month] += receipt['amount']

print("\nMonthly totals:")
for month in sorted(month_totals.keys()):
    print(f"{month}: {month_totals[month]:.2f}")

print(f"\nGrand total: {sum(month_totals.values()):.2f}") code
```

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
# Prepare the detailed expense data for Excel
import os
import re
from datetime import datetime

def extract_receipt_data(pdf_content, filename):
    """Extract data from taxi receipt PDF content"""
    # Extract amount using regex
    amount_match = re.search(r'Amount:\s*CNY\s*([\d.]+)', pdf_content)
    amount = float(amount_match.group(1)) if amount_match else 0.0
    
    # Extract date for month determination
    date_match = re.search(r'Date:\s*(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})', pdf_content)
    if date_match:
        date_str = date_match.group(1)
        date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
        month = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
    else:
        # Fallback: extract month from filename
        filename_date_match = re.search(r'receipt_(\d{8})_', filename)
        if filename_date_match:
            date_str = filename_date_match.group(1)
            date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y%m%d')
            month = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
        else:
            month = "Unknown"
    
    # Get filename without extension
    file_name_no_ext = os.path.splitext(filename)[0]
    
    return {
        'filename': file_name_no_ext,
        'month': month,
        'amount': amount
    }

# Complete list of all taxi receipts (excluding bus receipts)

 Verification QR Code
Note: This receipt is valid for business reimbursement'''),
    ('receipt_20250630_5.pdf', '''TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250630498564
Date:
2025-06-30
Time:
17:19
Passenger:
Zhang, Ming
Car Number:
BJ-D11925
Driver:
Wang, L.
Amount:
CNY 112.91
Service Provider: Shenzhou Car Service
 Verification QR Code
Note: This receipt is valid for business reimbursement''')
]

# Extract data from all taxi receipts
taxi_receipts = []
for filename, content in all_taxi_data:
    receipt_info = extract_receipt_data(content, filename)
    taxi_receipts.append(receipt_info)

# Sort by filename (which corresponds to chronological order)
taxi_receipts.sort(key=lambda x: x['filename'])

# Prepare data for Excel (3 columns: File_name, Month, Amount)
excel_data = []
for receipt in taxi_receipts:
    excel_data.append([receipt['filename'], receipt['month'], receipt['amount']])

print(f"Prepared {len(excel_data)} rows of data for Excel:")
print("First 5 rows:")
for i, row in enumerate(excel_data[:5]):
    print(f"  {i+1}. {row}")

print("...")
print("Last 5 rows:")
for i, row in enumerate(excel_data[-5:], len(excel_data)-4):
    print(f"  {i}. {row}")

# Save the data to a variable for use in Excel
print(f"\nTotal rows to write: {len(excel_data)}") code
```
